# <a name="msmq-custom-recipient-class"></a><span data-ttu-id="f7261-107">Класс "MSMQ-Custom-получател"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7261-107">MSMQ-Custom-Recipient class</span></span>
